<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гнедой.html>гнедо́й</a> (19048)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gnědъ</i>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">hnědý</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovak_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovak language">Slovak</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">hnedý</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гнедой.html>гнедо́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gnedój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>chestnut <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a horse</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гнедой.html>гнедо́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gnedój</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гнедой.html>гнедо́го</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гнедой.html>гнеды́е</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гнедой.html>гнеды́х</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>chestnut-colored horse</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>гне<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>до́й</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1b | .
<a href = vnd.unilang:краткий.html>Кра́ткая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рма</a> муж. р. <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:использоваться.html>испо́льзуется</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:образование.html>образова́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:остальной.html>остальны́х</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:краткий.html>кра́тких</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рм</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:затруднительный.html>затрудни́тельно</a>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гнездиться.html>гнезди́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gnezdítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to nest <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of birds</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to set up and live in a den <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of animals</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to huddle together, to live in crowded conditions <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of people</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to live in nests, to in large numbers <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of insects</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take root, to be present <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of thoughts or feelings</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gnězdo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*nisdós</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гнездо.html>гнездо́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gnezdó</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гнездо.html>гнезда́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гнездо.html>гнёзда</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гнездо.html>гнёзд</a></b>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гнести.html>гнести́</a> (31415)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gnestì</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gnet-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to press together</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gen-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to compress</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гнида.html>гни́да</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gnída</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гнида.html>гни́ды</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гнида.html>гни́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гнида.html>гни́д</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>nit <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">louse egg</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>scumbag, rascal</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:гнуть.html>гни́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> знач. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:гадкий.html>га́дкий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склоняться.html>склоня́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:образец.html>образцу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>существи́тельных</a> (<span title="в винительном падеже"><a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кого́</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a>?</span> — <i><a href = vnd.unilang:гнида.html>гни́ду</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:гнида.html>гни́д</a></i>).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-гнид-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***гнилой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гнилой.html>гнило́й</a> (6033)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gňilъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гнилой.html>гнило́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gnilój</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)гниле́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:гнилье.html>гниле́й</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">гниле́йший</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>rotten, putrid</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> damp <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of the weather or climate</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> weak, infirm</li></ol>

***гнить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гнить.html>гнить</a> (11461)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From Late <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gňìti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гнить.html>гнить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gnitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сгнить.html>сгнить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rot, to go bad, to putrefy, to decompose, to decay</li>
<li><i>teeth</i> to become carious</li>
<li><i>water</i> to stagnate</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гнусный.html>гну́сный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gnúsnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гнусность.html>гну́сность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gnúsnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гнусность.html>гну́сности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гнусность.html>гну́сности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гнусность.html>гну́сностей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>infamy, heinousness</li>
<li>heinous act</li></ol>

***гнусный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гнусный.html>гну́сный</a> (7057)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gnusьnъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гнусный.html>гну́сный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gnúsnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)гнусне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)гнусне́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>abominable, hideous, detestable, odious, vile
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:гнусный.html>гну́сная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:клевета.html>клевета́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>gnúsnaja</b> klevetá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">abominable slander</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:гнусный.html>гну́сная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ложь.html>ложь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>gnúsnaja</b> ložʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">vicious/filthy/rotten lie</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:гнусный.html>гну́сная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:погода.html>пого́да</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>gnúsnaja</b> pogóda</i> ― <span class="e-translation">foul/rotten weather</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:гнусный.html>гну́сная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́та</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>gnúsnaja</b> rabóta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">hateful job</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:гнусный.html>гну́сные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:шутка.html>шу́тки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>gnúsnyje</b> šútki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">filthy jokes</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>mean, villainous <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a person</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гнуть.html>гну́тый</a> (19478)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гнуть.html>гну́тый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gnútyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past passive imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гнуть.html>гнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:гнуть.html>гну́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>тый</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-г-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-ну-т</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гнуть.html>гнуть</a> (11282)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gъnǫti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гнуть.html>гнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:согнуть.html>согну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bend, to curve</li>
<li>to drive at, to aim at</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гнушаться.html>гнуша́ться</a> (23869)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гнус.html>гну́с</a>(ный)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gnús(nyj)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гнушаться.html>гнуша́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gnušátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to disdain, to abhor, to shun, to loathe</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:гнуть.html>гну́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ша́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — погнушаться.
<a href = vnd.unilang:участник.html>Уча́стники</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ситуация.html>ситуа́ции</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:описываемый.html>опи́сываемой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:помощь.html>по́мощью</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:гнушаться.html>гнуша́ться</a></i>: <img alt="NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3f/NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg/24px-NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg.png" decoding="async" width="24" height="24" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3f/NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg/36px-NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3f/NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg/48px-NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="75" data-file-height="75" /> <a href = vnd.unilang:субъект.html>субъект</a> (им. п.), <img alt="NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg/24px-NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg.png" decoding="async" width="24" height="24" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg/36px-NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg/48px-NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="75" data-file-height="75" /> <a href = vnd.unilang:объект.html>объект</a> (тв. п. <a href = vnd.unilang:либо.html>ли́бо</a> гл. <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> неопр. <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рме</a>).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-гнуш-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:говаривать.html>гова́ривать</a> (10272)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">govorítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говаривать.html>гова́ривать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">govárivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to say <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">repeatedly or frequently</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>; <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/iterative_aspect" class="extiw" title="w:iterative aspect">iterative</a> of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">govorítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:часто.html>ча́сто</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:говаривать.html>гова́ривал</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on částo <b>govárival</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he often used to say; he would often say</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>This is an iterative verb, and in standard language is conjugated only in the infinitive and the past tense.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:говно.html>говно́</a> (7985)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*govьno</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говно.html>говно́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">govnó</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говно.html>говна́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говно.html>го́вна</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говно.html>го́вен</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable<span class="ib-comma">,</span> vulgar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> shit</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vulgar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> shit, shitass, turd <i>(worthless person)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vulgar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> crap, junk <i>(worthless thing)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable<span class="ib-comma">,</span> vulgar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> bullshit <i>(nonsense)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:говно.html>говно́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:собачий.html>соба́чье</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>govnó</b> sobáčʹje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">dog shit (person or thing)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>Своё</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:говно.html>говно́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вонять.html>воня́ет</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Svojó <b>govnó</b> ne vonjájet!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">One’s own shit doesn’t stink!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>Не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тронуть.html>тро́нь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:говно.html>говно́</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вонять.html>воня́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бу́дет</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ne trónʹ <b>govnó</b>, a to vonjátʹ búdet!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Don't touch shit, because it will smell!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>гов<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но́</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:средний.html>сре́дний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1*d^  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>Встреча́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:написание.html>написа́ния</a> словоформы <i>им. п. мн. ч.</i>: <i>го́вны</i>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>Встреча́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:написание.html>написа́ния</a> малоупотребительной словоформы <i><a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>. п. мн. ч.</i>: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:говно.html>говн</a></i>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>Встреча́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:написание.html>написа́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>слова</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:принцип.html>при́нципу</a> «<i><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слышать.html>слы́шу</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:писать.html>пишу́</a></i>»): гавно.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-гов-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:порядочный.html>-н</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-о</b>.
</p>

Зализняка).

<p><b>гов<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но́</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:средний.html>сре́дний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1*d^  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>Встреча́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:написание.html>написа́ния</a> словоформы <i>им. п. мн. ч.</i>: <i>го́вны</i>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>Встреча́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:написание.html>написа́ния</a> малоупотребительной словоформы <i><a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>. п. мн. ч.</i>: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:говно.html>говн</a></i>.

***говор.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:говор.html>го́вор</a> (11473)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*govorъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говор.html>го́вор</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">góvor</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говор.html>го́вора</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говор.html>го́воры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говор.html>го́воров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> the sound of talking, the sound of voices, the sound of speech</li>
<li>murmur</li>
<li>dialect, patois</li>
<li>pronunciation, accent</li></ol>
